<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon&#8217;s First Quarter Net Earnings Climb 26.8 Percent on 15.3 Percent Sales Increase</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">First Quarter Highlights</font></font></div>

</td>
</tr></table>

<div>

</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">HUENENBERG, Switzerland &#8211; April 26, 2010 &#8211; </font>Alcon, Inc. (NYSE:ACL) reported that global sales rose 15.3 percent to $1.72 billion for the first quarter of 2010, or 9.6 percent excluding the impact of foreign exchange fluctuations and acquisitions.&#160;&#160;Revenue from acquisitions added 20 basis points to sales growth in the quarter.&#160;&#160;U.S. health care reform reduced sales by $5 million in the quarter.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Net earnings for the first quarter of 2010 grew 26.8 percent to $573 million, or $1.89 per diluted share, compared to $452 million, or $1.51 per diluted share in the first quarter of 2009.&#160;&#160;Non-GAAP adjusted net earnings would have grown 24.9 percent to $581 million, or $1.91 per diluted share, compared to first quarter 2009 non-GAAP adjusted net earnings of $465 million, or $1.55 per diluted share.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Adjusted net earnings in the first quarter of 2010 exclude a $24 million pre-tax reduction to cost of goods sold related to a change in estimate for accrued royalties, $4 million in pre-tax other operating expenses related to the potential change of control and merger proposal from Novartis AG and a $25 million period tax charge related to a change in the tax treatment of retiree medical benefits in the United States included in the health care reform bill.&#160;&#160;Adjusted net earnings in the first quarter of 2009 exclude $13 million of after-tax costs associated with a reduction in force.&#160;&#160;Reconciliations of reported and adjusted results for the first quarter are included in the financial tables below.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8220;Our first quarter results reflect another strong quarter with solid sales growth driven by continued market share gains in most major product categories, balanced contributions from all geographic regions and generally improved market conditions.&#160;&#160;Through the focused efforts of our entire organization, we also were able to translate that sales performance to faster growth in operating and net profit,&#8221; said Kevin Buehler, Alcon&#8217;s president and chief executive officer.&#160;&#160;&#8220;With this start to the year, we are on track to post solid results in 2010 that reflect sustainable organic growth and operational leverage.&#8221;</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Sales Highlights</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Summarized below are sales highlights for the first quarter of 2010. All growth comparisons are for the first quarter of 2010 compared to the first quarter of 2009. Organic sales growth rates exclude currency impacts and acquisitions and are non-GAAP measures that are reconciled in a table at the end of this release.</font></div>

ed States reduced contact lens care inventories on hand, which reduced sales in that quarter.</font></div>

</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Earnings Highlights</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Summarized below are earnings highlights for the first quarter of 2010. All growth comparisons are for the first quarter of 2010 compared to the first quarter of 2009.</font></div>

<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Wingdings">&#216;&#160;&#160;</font></div>
</td>
<td width="934">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Operating income rose 27.0 percent to $653 million, or 37.9 percent of sales.&#160;&#160;Non-GAAP adjusted operating income would have increased 19.0 percent to $633 million, or 36.8 percent of sales.&#160;&#160;This performance was attributable to strong sales growth, positive price contribution and SG&amp;A leverage resulting from the company&#8217;s on-going cost management programs.&#160;&#160;Adjusted operating income in the first quarter of 2010 excludes a $24 million pre-tax reduction to cost of goods sold related to a change in estimate for accrued royalties and $4 million in pre-tax other operating expenses related to the potential change of control and the merger proposal from Novartis.</font></font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FA
MILY: Times New Roman">&#160;Adjusted</font></div>
</div>
</td>
</tr></table>

<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">

<td align="right" style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Wingdings">&#216;&#160;&#160;</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Net earnings in the first quarter of 2010 rose 26.8 percent to $573 million, or $1.89 per diluted share.&#160;&#160;Non-GAAP adjusted net earnings would have risen 24.9 percent to $581 million, or $1.91 per diluted share.&#160;&#160;In addition to the increase in operating income, this solid performance included an improvement in earnings on the company&#8217;s investment portfolio and lower foreign exchange losses.&#160;&#160;Adjusted net earnings exclude the $21 million after-tax impact of the change in royalty estimates, $4 million in after-tax costs related to the potential change of control and the $25 million period tax charge related to health care reform in the United States.&#160;&#160;Adjusted net earnings in the first quarter of 2009 exclude $13 million in after-tax costs associated with a reduction in force.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Other Highlights</font></div>

<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><br>
<br>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Financial Guidance</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The company reaffirmed its full year guidance for both sales and earnings per share and said it expects to be able to absorb the ongoing impact of health care reform in its 2010 targets.&#160;&#160;Organic sales growth is expected to be in mid-to-high single digits, while earnings per share are expected to be in the range of $7.30 to $7.55.&#160;&#160;The on-going impact of health care reform is expected to reduce 2010 sales by $20 million and earnings per share by $0.06.&#160;&#160;The full year guidance assumes renewal of the U.S. Research and Experimentation tax credit in the fourth quarter of 2010 with retroactive application and excludes the adjustments made in the first quarter of 2010 and any future costs related to a potential change of control to and/or merger with Novartis.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Company Description</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon, Inc. is the world&#8217;s leading eye care company, with sales of approximately $6.5 billion in 2009.&#160; Alcon, which has been dedicated to the ophthalmic industry for 65 years, researches, develops, manufactures and markets pharmaceuticals, surgical equipment and devices, contacts lens solutions and other vision care products that treat diseases, disorders and other conditions of the eye.&#160; Alcon operates in 75 countries and sells products in 180 markets.&#160; For more information on Alcon, Inc., visit the Company&#8217;s web site at <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.alcon.com</font>.</font></div>
</div>
</div>

<td valign="top" width="2%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160; </font></td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">N/M - Not Meaningful</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Note: Change in constant currency calculates sales growth without the impact of foreign exchange fluctuations. Management believes constant currency sales change is an important measure of the company&#8217;s operations because it provides investors with a clearer picture of the core rate of sales growth due to changes in unit volumes and local currency prices.&#160;&#160;This measure is considered a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by Regulation G promulgated by the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Note: Adjusted operating income and net earnings measure the results of the company's operations without certain items that did not pertain to the comparable period. Management believes these measures are an important measure of the company&#8217;s operations because they provide investors with a clearer picture of the core operations of the company.&#160;&#160;These measures are considered non-GAAP financial measures as defined by Regulation G promulgated by the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission.</font></div>

<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Note: Organic change calculates sales growth without the impact of foreign exchange fluctuations and acquisitions. Management believes organic sales change is an important measure of the company&#8217;s operations because it provides investors with a clearer picture of the core rate of sales growth due to changes in unit volumes and local currency prices.&#160;&#160;This measure is considered a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by Regulation G promulgated by the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission.&#160;&#160;Certain reclassifications have been made to prior year amounts to conform to current year presentation.</font></div>
